A Dancing Girl's Large Belly: Bitter Lawsuit in Court 112

Zhao Xiuzhen Sues Zhu Mintang for Seduction, Demanding Over 70,000 Gold Pieces; Courtroom Filled with Laughter and Tears

Zhao Xiuzhen, a beautiful dancer from the Great Eastern Dance Hall, Zhao Xiuzhen is in her prime, with a pretty face. Although her figure is a bit thin, her proportions are just right, attracting the attention of many admirers.

Zhu Xiangjie, also known as Zhu Mintang, a comprador from Zhenhai, is young and good at business. He is currently a comprador for Yali Foreign Firm at 106 Sichuan Road. Last autumn, he frequented the dance hall and became involved with Zhao. Unfortunately, their good times didn't last, and their happy encounters ended midway.

The fruit was about to fall, but Zhao was already pregnant. Soon, she would be giving birth to a child without a father, which would be difficult for her. Zhao was unwilling to have lost her virginity to Zhu, so she hired lawyer Zhang Chongding to file a lawsuit against Zhu. Zhao's mother, Ms. Lu, listed herself as the plaintiff in her capacity as Zhao's legal guardian because Zhao was still a minor.

Many dancing girls were in the audience yesterday morning when the trial was scheduled to begin. The general public, especially the dancing girls, believed that this case was as important as the case of Huang Baiying and Tong Sanmao. Therefore, after 8 a.m., they called their friends and went to the Third Tribunal of the Special District Court to listen to the proceedings. The crowded situation was almost the same as when the Huang Baiying case was being heard.

After craning their necks for three hours, Zhao Xiuzhen and her mother arrived. Zhao was wearing a checkered red floral cheongsam, and her belly was as big as a five-stone gourd, which attracted even more attention. Presiding Judge Ge Zhiqin opened the court on time, but there were many other minor cases, and this case was scheduled last. It was not until 11:40 a.m. that this case was heard. Many dancing girls who came to listen to the proceedings did not get seats and craned their necks for three hours without showing any signs of fatigue, which showed their great concern.

Zhu Mintang, the defendant, did not appear. Lawyer E Sen represented him. Judge Ge first questioned the plaintiff mother and daughter about their age, place of residence, and then ordered the plaintiff's lawyer to state the grounds for the prosecution.

The charge of seduction was brought, and lawyer Zhang stood up and stated that the plaintiff in this case was prosecuting under Article 240, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law, the crime of seducing a woman under the age of 20. The plaintiff, Zhao Xiuzhen, was a dancer at the Great Eastern Dance Hall last year. In the autumn, the defendant, Zhu Mintang, entered the hall to dance, and the two met. From then on, the defendant often boasted to Zhao about his family's wealth and said that he was not yet married and wanted to marry Zhao. At that time, Zhao was only fifteen years old and was seduced by him.

There was physical contact. In December, they opened room 120 of the Great Eastern Hotel and had physical contact. On January 19 of this year, the defendant checked out of the hotel room and rented a house on Muir Ming Road and moved in together.

Showing photos of his wife and daughter. After some time, it was learned that the defendant was already married and had a daughter. The defendant did not hide this and showed Zhao photos of his wife and daughter together. Zhao's mother had allowed Zhao to live with the defendant. At this point, she revealed to her mother that the defendant already had a family.

After that, he disappeared and did not come. Zhao's mother valued old-fashioned morality and believed that a woman should be faithful to one man. Now that the matter was a foregone conclusion, she could only order her to retire to the position of concubine. However, the defendant was still not accommodating and said that since he already had a wife and children, it would be difficult to marry her again. From then on, he never came to Zhao's place, so she filed a lawsuit in the Special District.

73,000 yuan. As for the attached civil suit, Zhao is several months pregnant, and the future education and upbringing of the child will require funds, along with all current losses and Zhao's future living expenses, etc., for a total of 73,000 yuan to be paid by the defendant to the plaintiff.

The issue of publishing in the newspaper. Then, lawyer E stood up and stated that there was a preliminary issue in this case, which was also the direct reason why the defendant did not appear today. As soon as the plaintiff's statement was submitted, the summons had not yet been issued, and the trial date had not yet been set, but the newspapers had already published the content, which was the same as the plaintiff's statement. Who should bear the responsibility for this, the plaintiff's agent or the plaintiff? Because such a case involves public morals, not only should it not be disclosed arbitrarily in advance, but even if it is publicly tried, whether or not it should be announced is still up to the presiding judge to consider. Moreover, this case is purely the result of unsuccessful extortion. The defendant became angry and ill after seeing the report, so he could not come to court today. He then presented the doctor's certificate to the court. Judge Ge instructed lawyer E that he could directly investigate the source of the manuscript from the newspaper office regarding this point. There was no need to argue at this time.

The process of cohabitation. Then Zhao Xiuzhen was summoned to testify. According to her statement, she met the defendant at the Great Eastern Dance Hall in August last year. He repeatedly told me that his family was rich and unmarried, wanting me to follow him. I saw that his appearance was quite sincere and knew that he was only twenty-four years old, so I gave myself to him. We became intimate at the hotel on December 8, and on January 19, we moved to 37 Muir Ming Road. At this time, my mother also learned about it.

I am now eight months pregnant. Since moving in, all expenses have been provided by the defendant. He gives me an additional 150 yuan per month for the second, third, and fourth months. The defendant has repeatedly asked to get married formally, but has not done so. Later, I found out that he already had a wife and lived at 13 Lafayette Road, next door to Lafayette Fang. I have been pregnant for eight months.

Laughter from the audience. Judge Ge wanted to know her expression in addition to her pregnancy, so he ordered her to leave the witness stand and stand under the table for easy observation. Although Zhao had been in social circles for a long time and was used to everything, she couldn't help but blush when she heard the order in the courtroom. She had to shyly move and stand under the table. The onlookers laughed when they saw her big belly, but they immediately quieted down. Judge Ge ordered her to return to her original place.

Meeting with his wife. Continuing the questioning, she stated that the defendant had not come to my place since May and had not provided any living expenses, so the relationship broke down. Recently, I went to the defendant's house and met his wife. His wife is only twenty-three years old, literate, and has a good relationship with me. The defendant's parents and eldest daughter are all in Ningbo Shanghai residence, only one wife, one daughter, and male and female servants. Feeling pain and wanting to shed tears, she was asked in court whether she wanted to punish the defendant. Zhao replied that if he abandoned me, there must be a solution. If he doesn't abandon me, he should also explain. Therefore, I ask the court to make the decision. At this point, she felt something and tears were already welling up in her eyes. The judge's opinion. It was noon, and Judge Ge announced that in modern times, men and women have equal rights, and the law does not provide for the position of concubine. Regardless of whether the defendant's behavior should bear any legal responsibility, it is morally inappropriate. Now that the matter is a foregone conclusion, fortunately, the defendant's wife does not have any animosity towards the plaintiff, so there seems to be room for maneuver. The defendant is not present now and cannot proceed. He should be summoned again and the date changed to two weeks for questioning. If he still refuses to appear, he should be arrested. After the instruction, the court was adjourned.

Rejection of Dumb Love Case 113

Supreme Court's Third Instance Judgment

Lin Jimu, a 20-year-old deaf-mute residing in Sanle Li, Xingjia Muqiao, native of Zhongshan County, Guangdong Province, was found guilty of seducing a female compatriot, Wu Airong. He appealed to the Supreme Court against the first and second instance judgments sentencing him to two months of imprisonment with a three-year suspended sentence. The Supreme Court has already rejected the appeal. The judgment has been delivered in the past few days. Herewith is the full text of the Supreme Court's judgment. Supreme Court Criminal Judgment No. 811, 19th Year of the Republic of China (Judgment) Appellant Lin Jimu, male, 20 years old, native of Zhongshan County, Guangdong Province, residing in Sanle Li, Xingjia Muqiao, Shanghai, studying typing. The appellant appealed against the second instance judgment of the Jiangsu High Court on August 28, 18th Year of the Republic of China, in a case of obstructing family. The judgment of this court is as follows (Ruling) The appeal is rejected. The number of days Lin Jimu was detained before the judgment was finalized shall be deducted from the sentence at the rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. (Facts) Lin Jimu, whose ancestral home is in Guangdong, has been living in Shanghai. He became deaf and mute due to illness at the age of three. He has known Wu Guoshi's daughter, Wu Airong, from the same village since childhood. In the 18th year of the Republic of China, Wu Airong was 19 years old. During the first month of the lunar calendar that year, Lin Jimu lured her to his home and had sexual intercourse. On May 18 of the lunar calendar, he again had sexual intercourse with Wu Airong at the Da'an Hotel for four nights and then took her to his home to hide her. On May 27, Wu Guoshi met Lin Jimu on the road and asked about Wu Airong's whereabouts. Lin Jimu shook his head to indicate that she was not at his home. Wu Guoshi reported the matter to the police, who went to Lin Jimu's home and found Wu Airong and seized letters between Wu Airong and Lin Jimu. They were sent to the Shanghai District Court Prosecutor for investigation and prosecution. (Reasoning) The appellant's argument is that the appellant is a deaf-mute and has no ability to seduce, and that the appellant's purpose was to marry Wu Airong and should not constitute a crime. After investigation, Wu Airong was found by her mother and the police at the appellant's home. The appellant also confessed in the first instance that he had been having an affair with Wu Airong since the first month of this year and took her to the Da'an Hostel on May 18 for two days and then took her back home. He said, "I brought her here to be my wife." The original trial also provided roughly the same information. His seduction has been repeatedly admitted. Since it was not based on proper marriage procedures, he induced a woman under the age of 20 to leave her mother's supervision and repeatedly had sexual intercourse. The original judgment found that he had continuously intended to commit adultery and seduced her. In accordance with Article 75, Article 257, Paragraph 1 (the original judgment omitted Paragraph 1), Paragraph 2, and Article 33 of the Criminal Law, the sentence was reduced by six-fifths and sentenced to two months of imprisonment with a three-year suspended sentence. There is nothing inappropriate. The grounds for appeal are untenable. However, after investigation, the original judgment did not state the standard for deducting the number of days the appellant was detained during the investigation, nor did it record the reason for not allowing the deduction. According to the provisions of Article 324, Paragraph 4 of the Criminal Procedure Law, it is obviously inappropriate and should be corrected by this court ex officio. Based on the above arguments and conclusions, the judgment shall be made in accordance with Article 408, Paragraph 1 and Article 64 of the Criminal Law. Each main text of the Supreme Court Criminal Third Division Trial President Judge Ye Zaijun Judge He Yuquan Acting Judge Liu Shoulian Huang Wenhan Luo Qizhong Right Copy proves that it is identical to the original Clerk Liu Zhenfan

The Power Company Will Build a Commercial Radio Broadcasting Station 115

The Great American Evening News reported that according to Mr. Dai Le, General Manager of the Shanghai Power Company, the company will build a commercial radio broadcasting station in Shanghai next spring, using a kilowatt of power. The broadcasting range can reach all of China and the South Pacific islands of Japan. The Municipal Public Works Bureau Organizes the Bus Stops in Southern Shanghai 117

The stopping locations of the buses in Southern Shanghai along the tram tracks are generally close to the tram stops. Whenever two vehicles arrive at the station at the same time, other vehicles are blocked, which is detrimental to traffic. In view of this, the Municipal Public Works Bureau sent personnel to work with the Municipal Engineering Bureau to determine the locations where the buses should be relocated, and ordered the company to move them accordingly. Later, a deadline was set to urge the company to do so. The company then moved them according to the list, but at Laoximen, the original upward station was changed to the front of the house at No. 1438, and the downward station was changed to the front of the house at No. 1443. The company changed the upward bus to stop at No. 1465 and the downward bus to stop at No. 1458 for business reasons. After investigation by the Public Works Bureau and the Public Safety Bureau, for the sake of both traffic and business, they temporarily approved the trial operation. If it is found that it still hinders traffic in the future, it will be corrected again.

The Municipal Public Works Bureau Urges Inspection of High-Voltage Insulators 118

The high-voltage open-air switch insulator from Tiantong Road to Jixiang Road in Zhabei was previously damaged, causing a complete power outage in the area supplied by the Jixiang Road and Jiangwan substations for four hours. The Zhabei Water and Electricity Company sent workers to repair it. The Municipal Public Works Bureau reported that although the failure was caused by rain and the insulator breaking, the switch had been used for a long time without inspection, so the damage to the insulator was not detected. It happened that rainwater seeped into the cracks, and the wires were burned. The company could not shirk its negligence. Therefore, it ordered the company to inspect all insulators used for open-air switches and high-voltage overhead lines and replace them immediately if they were damaged to avoid the above failure from occurring again.

In addition to Wang Jiaxin being sentenced to two months of imprisonment for receiving stolen goods, Ji Zhongtang was found guilty of two counts of using violence and coercion to obtain confessions as a public official, and each was sentenced to one year of imprisonment. He was also found guilty of three counts of causing an innocent person to be prosecuted and punished as a public official, and each was sentenced to one year of imprisonment. He was also found guilty of one count of defrauding others of their property by means of fraud under the guise of his official authority, and three counts of attempting to do so, and each was sentenced to eight months of imprisonment. The sentence to be executed is three years of imprisonment and deprivation of political rights for six years as a warning.

Prohibit Books That Induce Gambling 128

Officials from the Chinese and Concession authorities, in view of the spread of the gambling disaster of flower clubs, and that women have gone bankrupt and committed suicide as a result of gambling, are now strictly prohibiting it. Ice Cream Boat Collides and Sinks 129

Xu Fulin Suffocates in the Boat

Meili Company has launched a boxed ice cream product. For days, they have sent people on gasoline boats to various wharves and ships to give away and sell it as an advertisement. The day before yesterday afternoon, they berthed at the Pudong Xinhui Mountain Wharf in North Huangpu. Unexpectedly, the Haiping Ship was exporting, causing the rear of the gasoline boat to be damaged, and the whole boat sank. At that time, there were five people who fell into the water, including the boss Wang Henggou, the old manager Wang Heshang, and Yi Wenxue Gong and Xu Fulin, who were sent by the company. However, the two Wangs and Yi Gong were all outside the cabin, so they were rescued when the boat sank, while Xu was in the middle cabin stocking goods, so when the boat sank, he could not get out and suffocated in the cabin. It was not until yesterday morning that the boat was salvaged, and Xu had suffocated to death inside. The head of the Weituoma Wharf Water Patrol Police Station ordered Detective Deng Jiagen to send the body to the South Wharf Life Saving Bureau and report to the local court. Prosecutor Yang and others went to the scene to verify and ordered the body to be buried.

Notice to Bicycle Riders 130

Prohibited from Riding in the Center of Tibet Road

Tibet Road is divided by boundary lines, and the central area, except for trams and automobiles, is strictly prohibited for all traffic. The Public Works Department has long issued this order, but bicycles and other vehicles still ride in the center, leading to tragic incidents such as being hit and crushed by cars. To prevent danger, the police have dispatched many patrol officers to Tibet Road. Anyone riding a bicycle or similar vehicle in the center will be taken to the police station and fined five dollars as a warning. This has already happened several times, each time involving more than a hundred bicycles. This morning, many bicycle riders were caught on Tibet Road, so cyclists must pay attention.

One Elderly Woman Dead, Two Workers Injured

Zhou and Zhu are both workers at the Nisshin Company. Around 4:15 AM, they were taken to Tongren Hospital by people in a vehicle for treatment. Desperate Young Man Jumps into Huangpu River 132

Silver Dollars Stolen, Hope of Returning Home Lost, Life at an End, He Takes This Last Resort

Yesterday morning around 6:00 AM, a very distressed young man on the Waibaidu Bridge at the mouth of the Suzhou River suddenly jumped into the river, intending to commit suicide. His body sank and then resurfaced a moment later. Fortunately, Chinese Constable No. 22 of the Water Police Station spotted him and immediately took action to rescue him, allowing him to live. He was taken to the police station, where he identified himself as Zhou Zhides, 23, from Shaoxing. On the 18th of this month, he left his hometown with 33 yuan for expenses to take the "New Beijing" ship to Shanghai. The ship ticket and other expenses cost him two yuan. Somehow, the remaining silver dollars were all stolen. After arriving in Shanghai, he tried to become a street vendor, but he was unable to because he had no capital. He was on the brink of starvation, and seeing no hope of returning home, he felt that death was his only option. After verifying his statement, the police chief ordered that he be held for investigation and disposal.

Case of Fraudulent Claim of May 30th Martyr's Compensation Settled Privately 133

Family Members Come to Testify, Luo Wenliang Apologizes in Court

The case of Wang Zhaohua and others using someone to fraudulently claim the compensation for the May 30th martyr Luo Wenzhao from the May 30th Family Association has been reported in previous newspapers after repeated summons by the Special District Local Court. Yesterday morning at 11:00 AM, the hearing continued. Family members Wu Shunbao, Yang Lianchun, Wang Dan, Hua Zonghai, Tang Tiansheng, Wang Zhou, Jiang Kuiyuan, Yao Tao, Zhan Chunting, Zhu Jinshan, Jin Zhou, Tan Yuanji, Wei Guoxiang, Chen Yongxing, Zhu Longfu, Yin Zhongshu, Wu Bingxun, and injured comrades Zhang Yueqiu, Qian Shishan, Chen Baoqing, Chen Tiemei, Shen Aqi, Zhang Huizhang, Wang Ada, Zou Baishan, George Ying, Monk Mei, Shi Hualang, Zhou Renlian, and others, a total of 36 people, all came to court to testify. At 10:30 AM, Presiding Judge Ge Zhitan ordered Xu Zhijian and Luo Wenliang to appear in court. First, Judge Ge questioned the plaintiffs, Hu Changsheng and Chen Fucai, about whether any progress had been made on the reconciliation during the one-week extension period. Hu and Xu stated that after discussing with Mr. Yu Qiaqing, chairman of the May 30th Board of Directors, reconciliation was possible, but Luo Wenliang had to publish an apology to the Family Association in the newspaper, and Xu Zhijian had to apologize to the Family Association. Judge Ge stated that the previous court hearing had urged the three parties to pay 500 yuan overseas to Luo Wen. The remaining amount could still be pursued after Wang Zhaohua and others were arrested. However, Xu Zhijian, the owner of Zhichengtai Tea Shop, replied that he was unable to pay the money. Judge Ge stated that since Xu claimed to be unable to pay, the case was difficult to reconcile. He then asked the two representatives, Hu and Chen, if the bank draft from He Lan Bank had been brought. Hu and Chen immediately produced the bank draft and presented it to the court. Judge Ge then questioned Xu Zhijian, asking if the seal on the back of the bank draft was from his store. Xu replied that it was not. He then asked if the seal on the insurance policy was from his store. Xu replied that it was, and that his daughter had it stolen and stamped on in the store. Judge Ge stated that the seal was still from his store, and that he was urging reconciliation to resolve the matter peacefully. At this point, Judge Ge asked the three parties' lawyers to discuss reconciliation among themselves. The case was adjourned until 2:20 PM when the court reconvened. After Judge Ge took the stand, he asked the three parties' lawyers if they could reconcile. Wu Chengyu, the lawyer representing the plaintiffs, stated the reasons why reconciliation was not possible. Zhang Xingyuan, the lawyer representing Luo Wenliang, stated that he was unwilling to publish an apology in the newspaper, but that Luo Wenliang had already drafted a version of the apology for reconciliation. He then presented the draft for review. After Judge Ge observed that the content of the draft contained an apology, he instructed lawyer Zhang Xingyuan, saying that since Luo Wenliang was willing to apologize, he would have Luo Wenliang apologize to the two representatives of the Family Association, Hu Changsheng and Chen Fucai, in court. Luo seemed unwilling. Judge Ge then stated that if he did not apologize, the Family Association would not give him a single penny since the procedures were correct. He then advised the two representatives, Hu Changsheng and Chen Fucai, to give Luo Wenliang an additional 50 yuan, for a total of 350 yuan. Hu and Chen both replied that they respected the court's decision and would comply. Judge Ge then ordered Xu Zhijian, the guarantor and owner of Zhichengtai Tea Shop, to pay 150 yuan, for a total of 500 yuan, to Luo. Xu initially repeatedly declined, claiming that the store was small and unable to pay. After Judge Ge repeatedly refuted him, Xu finally lowered his head and agreed to pay the amount. Judge Ge then ordered Luo to apologize to the two representatives, Hu and Chen, and taught him to say the eight words "I am sorry to you two." Luo then solemnly stated "I am sorry" to the two representatives, Hu Changsheng and Chen Fucai. Judge Ge then said that the three words "I am sorry" were even more sincere than an apology. He then wrote the reconciliation record in court and ordered the three parties to sign it. At the same time, he ordered Xu Zhijian to publish an advertisement in Shen Xinmin three newspapers, five lines each, thanking and apologizing to the two representatives of the Family Association, Hu Changsheng and Chen Fucai. Xu agreed, and the court announced that the court was adjourned. At this point, the reconciliation was reached.

Continued Report on the Collision Between the Daji and Jiangjing 134

The collision between the Daji and Jiangjing轮 has been briefly reported in yesterday's newspaper. The following is a detailed report on the true situation of the accident and the extent of the damage:

Location of the collision: The China Merchants Bureau's Jiangjing轮 was sailing downstream from Hankou. Most of the passengers on board disembarked in Nanjing. At 5:30 AM on the 22nd, when the ship reached Baimaisha, below Tongzhou, the river surface was narrow. The Dada Company's Daji轮 was approaching from behind, also heading towards Shanghai. The Daji船 was smaller and faster and eager to overtake. The captain of the Jiangjing船, Crowf, thought the river surface was too narrow and warned the Daji轮 to slow down for fear of danger. However, the Daji轮 continued to speed up and rush forward. When the Daji轮 attempted to pass the Jiangjing轮, the stern of the Daji轮, due to the limited space between the two ships, was unable to avoid the Jiangjing轮 and crashed into the bow of the Jiangjing轮 with a loud bang, causing the accident.

Extent of the damage: When the Jiangjing轮 was hit, it was just dawn and all the passengers on board were fast asleep. The sudden impact made everyone think they had run aground. Passengers in the middle and rear cabins rushed to the deck. The captain explained that it was a collision and that there was no danger, and everyone was relieved. The collision occurred on the starboard bow. Due to the force of the impact, the outer hull was damaged, and all six berths in the forward cabin were destroyed. At that time, four stokers were sleeping in the berths and were thrown from the berths, suffering head injuries and bleeding profusely. Two people on the lower level were almost crushed to death. Fortunately, there were no passengers in the cabin, so no lives were lost. The railings and iron pillars on the upper deck were also broken, with about five or six zhang of damage. Fortunately, the damage was above the waterline. The stern of the Daji轮 also had its outer hull plates dented. The damage was not as extensive as that of the Jiangjing轮.

What happened after the accident: After the accident, the Daji轮 arrived in Shanghai first, followed by the Jiangjing轮. Both ships reported to the customs for inspection. Due to schedule constraints, they each repaired the damage separately and will investigate the responsibility for the accident later. Yesterday, the Daji轮 was already in the dock for repairs to its stern. The Jiangjing轮 is still docked at the Jinliyuan Wharf and must wait for the engineering committee of the shipping department to inspect the ship before it can be sent to the factory for repairs. It is estimated that it will be delayed for ten days before the repairs are completed and the ship can set sail.

American Drops Notes, Commits Assault, Negotiations Ensue 135

Breaks Yang Qifa's Ring Finger, Falsely Reports Armed Police Occupying Ship

Yang Qifa, a 32-year-old man from Yangzhou, is proficient in English. Whenever American merchant ships arrive in port, Yang would board the ship to exchange domestic notes for American notes with the Americans. He exchanged about three yuan of domestic notes for one yuan of American notes. Yang would then take the American notes to a money shop to exchange them back into domestic currency. As a result, he could earn a profit of several angles per yuan. The amount of money he earned each time was quite considerable, and Yang used this as a business. On the morning of the 20th of this month, around 10:00 AM, Yang was soliciting business on the American ship "Jinxiang," which was docked in the Huangpu River. An American man took out twenty yuan in American notes and made a deal with Yang. Yang then paid him sixty-four yuan in domestic notes. The American man complained that the amount he was paid was too little and argued with Yang. Yang said that if he was unwilling, he could return the money. The American man heard this and became furious, using force and savagery. He broke the ring finger of Yang's right hand and then stabbed Yang's right cheek with a sharp blade. Yang was injured and bleeding profusely. Yang cried out for help in extreme pain. All the notes and money he was carrying, forty yuan in large notes and forty-one angles in small notes, were taken away. At that time, Jia Tianxi and other team members of the Fourth Team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau's Water Patrol Team were patrolling the river and heard the cries. They immediately jumped on board the ship to investigate the cause. The American man saw the police arrive and panicked, hiding in the cabin. On the spot, the police rescued Yang and took him to a sampan boat. The boatmen there advised Yang not to make a fuss, lest he be bullied by foreigners in the future and cause trouble. Yang then went ashore, took a car, and went to a hospital near Tilanqiao for medical treatment. After the incident, the American man used the telephone to report to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, falsely claiming that a large number of armed police were occupying the American ship "Jinxiang" and requesting that police be sent to rescue them. Director Yuan immediately ordered the Water Patrol Corps to investigate. Captain Xu of the corps obeyed the order and dispatched Patrol Officer Wang to lead several police officers to the scene by speedboat. They boarded the ship and investigated, but there were no armed police in sight. They then went to the Fourth Team to investigate what had happened. Jia and other officers explained the situation. Captain Xu of the corps heard the report and, considering the seriousness of the matter, yesterday specially summoned Yang Qifa for a preliminary hearing. Yang immediately confessed the whole story. The captain believed that the American man on the ship had committed the assault, stabbed Yang, robbed his money, and then fabricated a false report, treating the police like children. The captain immediately prepared a document to be submitted to Director Yuan of the Municipal Public Security Bureau for instructions.

Opening of the Minhang Public Medical Clinic 140

Minhang Town, in the first district of Shanghai County, is the leading town in Shanghai County. Its location is strategic, and its population is dense. Its district administration and the rectification of market travelers can be called a model for rural areas. Recently, the town district office, charity groups, and others, considering the extreme heat of this year's summer and the susceptibility to epidemics in the autumn, and that poor people who contract diseases often have no means to seek medical treatment, endangering their lives, specially discussed with the Puan Charity Hall Medical Association to organize a public medical clinic to provide regular medical treatment without charging consultation fees. The clinic is located in the Puan Charity Hall, which has spacious rooms and good ventilation. The clinic is equipped with all departments and has everything it needs. The clinic is well-organized and orderly. It officially opened yesterday, and those seeking treatment are constantly coming. The general public praises the clinic's public welfare.

The tenants of Yile Lane on Tangshan Road in Hongkou, Shanghai, were suddenly notified that their rent would be increased by one-third. The tenants of the lane believe that in Shanghai, where life is becoming increasingly difficult, many families are struggling to provide food and clothing. Now, the landlord has suddenly increased the rent, and the amount of the increase is beyond what is reasonable. The rise and fall of labor strikes are the cries of your unbearable oppression and exploitation, and have drawn the sympathy and boundless admiration of 120,000 fellow workers in all industries in Shanghai. The workers of the Japanese-owned Hua Sha Textile Mill in Pu Dong, unable to endure the rising cost of living, have risen up to demand improved treatment and increased wages to sustain their livelihood, which is a reasonable and legitimate request. However, the Japanese capitalists have brazenly and unreasonably refused. As a result, all the workers have been forced to strike and persist in their struggle for nearly a month. The Japanese capitalists have not only refused to accept the conditions, but have also threatened to close the factory and secretly recruited new workers, plotting to resume production. The Japanese capitalists' conspiracies and malicious schemes are emerging one after another, and the workers' suffering is deepening day by day. Our union firmly believes that the impact of this strike by the workers of the Japanese-owned Hua Sha Textile Mill in Pu Dong is not only the fate of the 3,000 workers in that factory, but also the life and death of 53,000 workers in all Japanese-owned textile mills in Shanghai. The strike by the workers of the Japanese-owned Hua Sha Textile Mill in Pu Dong is a vanguard of the entire team, so our union must awaken the deep attention of all the workers in Japanese-owned textile mills, and even more so, warn all the workers of the Japanese-owned Hua Sha Mills Three and Four and Xi He Mills One and Two in Pu Xi, who have close ties with the workers of the Japanese-owned Hua Sha Mill in Pu Dong, to provide sympathetic assistance as soon as possible. Dear workers, your past failures and all the suffering you have endured are due to the lack of mutual assistance. This time, you must quickly and fully develop your instinct for mutual assistance and help each other. Do not think that the strike in one factory is the business of the workers in that factory and ignore it. No matter which factory you work in, you must regard each other as brothers. If one brother is in trouble, everyone should unite to help. Only in this way can you subdue the Japanese capitalists and achieve final victory. Let us all enthusiastically shout slogans: Unite all textile mill workers in Shanghai to jointly assist the strike of the workers of the Japanese-owned Hua Sha Textile Mill in Pu Dong to increase wages and improve treatment! Support the Shanghai Special Municipality Textile Mill Industry Workers Union Preparatory Committee.

Letter to the Editor 145

To the esteemed editor, I recently read the news in your paper about the French Concession strictly prohibiting flower arrangement organizations, including the phrase "Wang A'er, No. 32, Fill in the words of the Eight Immortals, established a flower arrangement organization." This is actually a mistake for No. 31. I, the writer, have lived at No. 32 for many years, and the several families living here are all legitimate merchants. I am truly afraid that distant relatives and friends will be concerned by the rumors. Therefore, I am sending this letter to correct the error and hope that it will be published in the "Letters to the Editor" column. Sincerely, Xu Xiaoyun, August 23.

Recording the 13th Annual Conference of the Chinese Institute of Engineers (1) 146

The Grand Opening at Northeastern University in Shenyang

(Shenyang Correspondence) The 13th annual conference of the Chinese Institute of Engineers opened on the 18th at the College of Science and Engineering of Northeastern University. The opening ceremony was extremely grand. The details of the conference are recorded below:

Attendees Approximately 3,000 members of the Chinese Institute of Engineers nationwide. Most were unable to attend due to transportation difficulties and reported by letter. Only a small number of those attending arrived on the 16th and 17th to register. The attendees included Dai Jizheng from the Hangzhou Branch (reportedly), Gao Dagang, Yao Chang'an, Gu Daosheng, and Cai Xiong from the Nanjing Branch, Zhang Sheying, Yu Gaomin, Du Deisan, and Lu Zhishun from the Jinan Branch, Ri Yuanguang from the Tianjin Branch, Wang Jixu from the Beiping Branch, Guo Keti, Wang Xiaohua, Chen Fangtao, Yu Chichang, Liu Xianzhou, Feng Zhudi, Zhou Youyan, Zou Tong, Sun Guofeng, Zhao Jichang, Yu Qianliu, Peng Kaixu, Guan Chenglie, Zhao Shenshu, Pan Chengxiao, Xue Guilin, Lei Huan, Du Dianying, Yu Zhihe, Zhang Jie, Wang Xu, Wang Hanchen, Lin Sicheng, Xing Dao, Zhang Wanfa, Lu Junhe, Xu Qingchun, Zhang Shixing, Li Weicheng, Wang Huatang, Lu Bangxing, and Zhang Xiangyu from the Shenyang Branch, Tao Ludun, and others, totaling 46 people. There are still members en route who will arrive within the next few days. Zhang Xueliang's representative Wu Jiaxiang, Northeast Military Police Commander Chen Xingya's representative Li Hongming, Minister of Agriculture and Mining Liu Heling's representative Wen Jiao, Construction Director Peng Jiqun, Education President Wang Hua-yi, Yao Jin-sheng, Liao Ning-fang Yarn Factory Manager Sun Zuchang, Shen Hai Railway Company Associate Chen Shutang, General Chamber of Commerce Vice President Lu Nai-geng, North China Machinery Factory Director Liu Shaoba, Chinese Mining and Metallurgical Engineering Society Representative Xue Guilin, Northeast Mining Society Representative Zhao Rentao, Northeast Cultural Society Representative Feng Wuyue, and others also arrived.

Opening Ceremony The opening ceremony was announced at 10 AM. After the ceremonial rites, the first speech was given by Wang Xiaohua, the chairman of the Shenyang branch, who briefly stated that today is the first day of the 13th annual conference of the Chinese Institute of Engineers. He was honored by the presence of guests from all walks of life. Due to the disruption of the Beining Railway, very few members from Pinghan have arrived. In addition, the Shenyang branch has not been re-established for long and has not been able to make sufficient preparations. He hoped that everyone would forgive him. Next, representatives from various branches reported [T13]One[/T] Jinan briefly stated that last year the branch had only 28 members, but now it has increased to more than 80. The branch affairs are very developed. Meetings are held once a week. Recently, due to local martial law, meetings have not been held for two months. Almost all engineering figures from various factories and industrial organizations in Jinan are members of the branch. The branch often plans engineering matters for local organizations and has contacted the government about obtaining a meeting place. [T13]Two[/T] Beiping briefly stated that in the past, the branch had many members, but since the capital moved south, the number of members has greatly decreased and the addresses of the members are mostly unknown. The branch directors have also mostly left Beiping and the meetings are very few. This time, many members planned to come to Shenyang to participate in the annual conference, but due to the Beining Railway traffic being blocked, very few have arrived. Some are still on the way but have not yet arrived. [T13]Three[/T] Very few members from Shanghai have arrived due to transportation difficulties.

Guests' Speeches First, Education Director Wu Jiaxiang read the Commander's congratulatory message. Then, Construction Director Peng Zhiqun, Education Director Wu Jiaxiang, and Northeastern University Representative Sun Guofeng, Dean of the College of Science and Engineering, gave speeches. Then, Xue Guilin, representative of the Chinese Mining and Metallurgical Engineering Society and the Northeastern Mining Society, gave a speech stating that China's territory can be divided into two major parts: one is the eleven provinces and the other is the border region. Three-quarters of China's area is the border region, and the border region accounts for one-seventh of the country's population. The three northeastern provinces account for 10% of the country's area and 5% of the population. Heilongjiang is the second largest province in the country, but the population is very small. Jingbo Lake has 400,000 kilowatts of hydropower, and there are many gold mines in Heilongjiang. Today, China will change to the gold standard, so it is necessary to open gold mines. The responsibility for developing the border region lies with the engineering community. The Hinggan Mountains and Ronglu Island are being developed. Jingbo Lake has 400,000 kilowatts of hydropower, and there are many gold mines in Heilongjiang. In the 18th year of the Republic of China, a Japanese investigation team of 361 groups, with 15,266 people, entrusted Nankai School to establish the Northeast Research Association, and Tsinghua School also established the Chinese Border Research Association. Last year, the Nanjing government also sent people to the east to investigate. Russians have detailed investigations into Xinjiang, and the British have detailed investigations into Tibet. He hoped that the Institute of Engineers would pay attention to the Chinese border region and work hard to develop it. Finally, the chairman gave a reply. The meeting adjourned at 12 noon.

Matters for discussion The business meeting continued at Beiling at 2 PM. Matters for discussion: Liu Zengmian requested to compile and issue Chinese engineering books as soon as possible. It was resolved that the Institute of Engineers should contact major bookstores and notify members that all completed and upcoming works must be submitted to the Institute for review. In addition, rules for soliciting manuscripts will be set separately. The meeting adjourned at 5:30 PM and went to Zhongxintang Restaurant on Sanjing Road for dinner (19th). Huanhua

Chen Shizhen Concurrently Appointed as Director of the Social Affairs Department 147

Gu Shusen Concurrently Serves as Acting Director of the Mongolian and Tibetan Education Department

Chen Jian, Director of the Department of Social Education and concurrent Director of the Department of Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs of the Ministry of Education, has resigned. This was reported in yesterday's (22nd) newspaper. The Ministry of Education submitted a request to the Executive Yuan and then to the National Government to appoint Chen Shizhen, counselor of the Ministry, as Director of the Department of Social Education, and Gu Shusen, Director of the Department of General Education, as Acting Director of the Department of Mongolian and Tibetan Education. The reporter interviewed Director Chen at the Ministry. According to Chen, the scope of social education is very broad and, in a broad sense, includes the entire education system. In terms of the current undertaking of the Department of Social Education, it is people's education, so he believes that if (Social Education) is changed to (People's Education), it would be more appropriate, but it is not the most appropriate name. He feels that he is physically weak and may not be able to handle the heavy responsibilities of the Department of Social Affairs. Now that he has repeatedly resigned and has not been allowed, he has to temporarily serve concurrently and requested that Minister Jiang carefully select a social education expert to take this seat, so that he can continue to serve as a counselor.

Ministry of Education Interprets Doubts About Religious Groups Running Educational Undertakings 148

According to the Zhejiang Education Department, the Ministry of Education received a report from Dongyang, Lishui, and other counties regarding the method of religious groups running educational undertakings and requested instructions. The Ministry of Education has already made provisions in the previously issued Announcement No. 7. Now, the Ministry is further explaining the meaning of the word "organization" in the second item and instructing the Zhejiang Education Department: "The Ministry has learned that the second item of Announcement No. 7 of the Ministry refers to the meaning of the word 'organization' when a religious group establishes an organization to propagate its faith. It refers to churches, temples, or societies and training centers established by followers of each religion for preaching and lecturing, with the aim of teaching religious doctrines. If they cleverly set up names to recruit school-age children to teach elementary school subjects or various miscellaneous characters, which are obviously school properties, they should follow the regulations for private schools. As for the request in the report that boys and girls under the age of thirteen should not be allowed to attend lectures in religious organizations for propaganda, it is not appropriate to explicitly prohibit this before the cancellation or amendment of the Sino-Foreign Missionary Treaty. However, boys and girls under the age of thirteen are in the period of receiving national education and should be ordered by the education bureaus of each city and county to send their fathers and brothers to nearby elementary schools to receive formal national education, so as to avoid being influenced by the doctrines of one religion at a young age when they are still shallow and have no ability to choose. Please follow these instructions and forward them to be followed."

Comparison of the Number of Elementary School Children in Various Counties in Jiangsu Over the Years 149

The number of elementary school children in various counties in Jiangsu over the years has been reported in previous newspapers. Now, the Jiangsu Provincial Preparatory Office for Compulsory Education has compiled the statistics of the elementary school children in various counties in Jiangsu from the beginning of the Republic of China to June of the 18th year of the Republic of China. The key points of the seventeen years are extracted below:

[T13]One[/T] The total number of children in each county during the seventeen years increased from 200,456 (the first year of the Republic of China) to 507,644 (the 17th year of the Republic of China), an increase of 307,188, which is two and a half times the number of children in the first year of the Republic of China. On average, the number of children increased by 8,070 per year. [T13]One[/T] The closer to the present year, the more children increased. For example, in the second year, the number of children increased by 1,111, while in the 17th year, the number of children increased by 42,057, which is almost four times the number of children in the second year. [T13]One[/T] Although the number of children generally increased year by year, the number of children increased in each year varied greatly. The increase rate was the largest in the 17th year, followed by the 15th year, the 4th year, and the 10th year. However, the number of children increased in the 5th, 8th, and 12th years was less than the number of children in the previous year. [T13]One[/T] The number of children increased every year, but in the 15th year, the number of children suddenly decreased by 78,504, which is about the same as the number of children increased from the first year of the Republic of China to the 5th year of the Republic of China. This one-year setback cancelled the five-year increase. This was due to military influence. After the military was pacified, Nanjing and Shanghai were designated as special municipalities and were no longer included in the statistics. [T13]One[/T] Comparing the situation in each county, there were 13 counties with less than 1,000 children in the first year of the Republic of China, but only Yangzhou in the 17th year. And the number of children has increased from 34 to 851, an increase of more than 25 times. [T13]One[/T] In the first year of the Republic of China, the counties with more than 10,000 children were Shanghai, Wujin, and Wuxi. By the 17th year, there were 16 counties and cities: Wujin, Wuxi, Yancheng, Nantong, Rugao, Shanghai, Jiangyin, Changshu, Yixing, Haimen, Chongming, Tongshan, Jiading, Songjiang, Taixing, and Suzhou. [T13]One[/T] In total, the county with the fewest number of children in the seventeen years was Yangzhou with 34, and the county with the most number of children was Wujin with 27,682 (excluding Shanghai, Nanjing Special Municipality, and Suzhou City). [T13]One[/T] The increase rate of the number of children is mostly faster in counties with fewer children than in counties with more children. The number of children increased more in recent years of the Republic of China than in the early years. [T13]One[/T] A special situation is that the number of children suddenly decreased by 78,504 in the 15th year. Generally, the more children there were, the more children decreased. The most severe were Wuxi, Shanghai, and Jiangning, followed by Xuhai area in Jiangbei. [T13]One[/T] The increase difference is very large. For example, comparing the 16th and 17th years, Yizheng increased by 5 children, while Haimen increased by 7,219 children. The decrease difference is also very large. For example, in the same year, Wujiang decreased by 2 children, while Taixing decreased by 9,887 children. [T13]One[/T] There was no county with only increases and no decreases in the seventeen years. For example, Rugao, Nantong, and Jingjiang (only one year decreased). There was no year with only increases and no decreases (the counties with decreases in the 4th and 8th years were relatively few).

Ms. Zhang Xiaomei Returns Home After Completing Her Studies 153

Ms. Zhang Xiaomei, the daughter of Mr. Zhang Changfu, the Chinese Manager of Pathé Records in this city, is naturally intelligent and studious. In 1926, she graduated from Ginling Women's College in Nanjing with a Bachelor of Arts degree in Social Economics. In the autumn of that year, she went to the United States to study at the University of Chicago, obtaining a Master of Arts degree in the same field in 1927. She then passed the entrance exam for the University of London in England. In 1929, she transferred to the University of Geneva in Switzerland and entered the Graduate Institute of International Studies, continuing her research in Social Economics. This summer, after a rigorous examination by the institute, she was recognized for her outstanding academic performance and was officially awarded a doctorate. Ms. Zhang has already purchased a boat ticket to return to China, having accepted a position at the Bank of China. The Graduate Institute of International Studies in Geneva is known as a gathering place for the most renowned professors from various European countries, making its standards higher than any other academic institution. Ms. Zhang is the first person to receive a doctorate in Social Economics from the institute. Many European newspapers have published articles about this event, considering it an unparalleled honor for China.

Sports

Rotary Cup Semi-Finals, Act Two 154

Today at 4 PM. Yesterday England won all three sets straight against the United States in the singles match. Today England and the United States will have another singles match.

Yesterday's second act of the Rotary Cup International Tennis Semi-Finals featured doubles matches between China and Portugal, and England and the United States. The audience was still very enthusiastic. The England-United States match was considered the most important, as both countries needed to win the doubles match to secure a spot in the finals. The United States team consisted of Squire and Budge, while the English team was composed of Wheatley and Stock. Comparatively, the United States' strength was far behind. Budge was originally an experienced player, but he had just arrived in Shanghai the night before at 9 PM after escaping the summer heat in Qingdao. Not only was he exhausted from the journey, but he had also been out of practice for a long time. Therefore, his performance yesterday was extremely weak, with frequent errors and no brilliance. Squire also performed mediocrely. Wheatley of England, on the other hand, is a veteran with many years of experience and received help from Stock. They defeated the United States by a score of three to zero. The Chinese team, Zheng Zhaojia and Jiang Daozhang, faced Portugal's Canavaro and Colasa. Both sides were evenly matched and evenly matched. The match started at 4:15 PM and continued until 6:50 PM. The sky was already dark, and the lights were on, but the winner had not yet been determined. The score was two sets each, with eight games each. The match was adjourned and will be resumed today.

(1) England Wins Singles Against the United States 155

(England) Wheatley and Stock 6-3, 6-2, 6-2 Squire and Budge (United States)

The England-United States match started first. The United States team appeared weak from the start, especially Budge. The English team easily won three games in a row. In the fourth game, Squire of the United States served and initially showed no signs of improvement. After another failure, he worked hard to win the game. The score then became 4-1, 4-2, and 5-3. In the end, England won 6-3. In the first game of the second set, the United States won. England's momentum was fierce, and they soon won 3-1, then 3-2. England then went on to win 6-2. The third set was also 6-2. In total, England won 3-0.

(2) Chinese-Portuguese Doubles Tie 156

(China) Zheng Zhaojia and Jiang Daozhang 6-4, 3-6, 2-6, 6-3, 8-8 Canavaro and Colasa (Portugal)

The Chinese-Portuguese match was very intense, and the audience was extremely excited. The outcome was crucial to the overall situation. If China won, they would secure a spot in the finals. If Portugal won, the score would be 2-1, and the finals spot would depend on the final singles match. After alternating victories, China won the first two games. The Portuguese team was also strong and unwilling to fall behind. They fought fiercely, and the score soon became 2-1 and 3-3. The first set ended with China winning 6-4. In the second set, the Portuguese team gained an advantage and advanced to win 6-3. The Portuguese team's momentum suddenly increased, and Zheng and Jiang of China made more mistakes. The Portuguese team then won another game 6-2. In these three sets, Zheng and Jiang's performances were comparable, with both strengths and weaknesses. From the fourth set onwards, Jiang Daozhang suddenly appeared weak, with many self-inflicted errors. Zheng Zhaojia, on the other hand, suddenly showed his characteristics, with his net play and passing shots becoming even more impressive. In the fourth set, China lost first but then won, eventually winning 6-3, making the score two sets each. In the fifth set, both sides had to intensify their efforts, and the score was often tied, making it difficult to determine the winner. The score became 2-2, then 4-4, then 5-5, then 6-6, 7-7, and finally 8-8. The audience was captivated by the back-and-forth play. In the end, due to the late hour, a final victor could not be decided, and the match was adjourned.

(3) Matches Continue Today 157

Starting at 4 PM

The Chinese-Portuguese doubles match, which did not determine a winner yesterday, will be cancelled by agreement of both sides. Today at 4 PM, the match will be replayed to determine the victor. In addition, England's Wheatley and the United States' Squire will play a singles match. Both matches will start at 4 PM.

A Laughing Matter 163

— Hai Ke

A: I heard that your wife is seeing a doctor to lose weight because she's too fat. Has it been effective?

B: It's all a scam. It hasn't been effective at all.

A: But I saw your wife yesterday, and she seemed a little thinner.

B: Hmm, that's because she wasted a lot of money for nothing. She's depressed, so she lost weight.

Husband: Honey, what do you think of my little brother? Isn't he adorable?

Wife: Yes, very adorable. Just like his older brother. It's just a pity he's too young.

A: Look at this photo. I'm taking a picture with two police dogs. It was taken in Paris. Can you recognize me?

B: They're almost the same. It's hard to tell. Is that you in the middle with the hat?

A Child: What are you drawing there?

B Child: I'm drawing a cow.

A Child: But where are the horns?

B Child: They're still in the inkwell. They haven't come out yet.

A: Old friend, why do you look so terrible? It's like you've been sentenced to life imprisonment.

B: Maybe I have. Because I got engaged to Miss C the day before yesterday.

Juyuan Notes 164

— Tianxu Wosheng

Yesterday, a gentleman I did not know sent me a letter asking me to devise a solution to his current livelihood problems. He is currently a foreman in a sock factory with a monthly salary of only ten yuan. He has four children, and his wife cannot work because she is breastfeeding an infant, etc. I thought about it all evening and got up at dawn to draft this hypothetical plan, which seems quite feasible. It is indeed a practical problem for one person to earn ten yuan a month and try to support a family of six. Fortunately, he has not yet reached the point of having no place to stand and still has this monthly income of ten yuan, which is better than being unemployed and sitting idly by. I believe that since his wife cannot work due to breastfeeding the infant, the first solution should be to foster the child in the home of a villager for four or five yuan a month. His wife can then work as a nanny for someone else while she still has milk, earning ten yuan a month. The cost of food and lodging will be provided by the other household, which will lighten the burden. The ages of the other three children are unknown. If they are all breastfed, then, according to physiological norms, she should not become pregnant while she is lactating. The eldest child should be over ten years old and should be taken into the factory to work as an apprentice. This will provide for the child's food and lodging, further lightening the burden. The second and third children should be sent to kindergarten or fostered in other people's homes for only ten yuan a month. He can then ask the factory owner to allow him a place to sleep in the factory. This will increase his working hours and effort, and his monthly salary should naturally increase. Even in the current situation, the couple's monthly income is twenty yuan. Subtracting the fifteen yuan for the children's expenses, there should be five yuan left for savings. In case of illness, there will be enough for ordinary hospitalization. Therefore, there is no need to rent a house. Since he lives in the factory, he can concentrate on his work and consider everything his responsibility, sharing weal and woe with the factory. This will earn him the trust of the factory owner, who will promote him to an important position and rely on him. Within three years, he may become the factory director or manager. Although he may feel sad about the temporary separation from his family, he will not have the worry of six mouths starving and freezing. With the burden eased, he will have the hope of advancement in three years, and his spirits will be lifted. Even if he remains in his old position, his salary will naturally increase with his service. After three years, he should be able to earn at least ten yuan more per month, and he will have savings for education expenses. Life is about being content with one's circumstances and living within one's means. Why should he end up like a wandering minister of Chu, starving his wife and children? If his wife is unwilling to work as a nanny, then one loom in the home and the two children can cook together, and they will not be in a desperate situation. However, this will be much more laborious than the ease of working as a nanny. I am afraid that if they become slightly more comfortable, and she gives birth to a fifth child, they will return to their original state, only increasing their burden and suffering. I must do my best to advise people, so I offer this additional advice. I cannot remember the gentleman's address, so I am writing this in my notes and sharing it with others who have similar problems.

Tragic News of Suicide in West Lake 165

— Qiulang

He committed suicide in frustration after failing to obtain a government position and being scammed out of borrowed money.

Recently, people in Shanghai, faced with the pressure of life or changes in their love life, have often resorted to jumping into the Huangpu River as their final destination. The sadness and misery of the situation, with life being treated like a feather, is truly lamentable. Unexpectedly, this trend has recently spread to Hangzhou. In that scenic and tranquil place, someone recently committed suicide by drowning in West Lake. After sighing, I secretly wonder why the beautiful and gentle West Lake has suddenly turned into a ferocious beast devouring people. I will now describe what I have heard:

A man named Tang, from Sheng County, graduated from a certain middle school. However, he was naturally pedantic and did not know how to produce anything. He spent his days reading and chanting, which led to the decline of his family's wealth. Recently, he became obsessed with officialdom and heard people say that becoming a county magistrate was easy and a shortcut to making money. He wrote a letter to a friend in Hangzhou, Mr. Jia, asking him to help him get a recommendation. Jia was working in a certain agency in Hangzhou. After receiving Tang's letter, he knew that Tang was foolish and could be deceived. A few days later, he sent back a letter falsely claiming that he had taken care of everything and that Tang had been appointed as the county magistrate of Lin'an County by order of so-and-so. He asked Tang to quickly raise a certain amount of money and bring it to Hangzhou so that he could take office. Tang was overjoyed upon receiving the letter. He hurriedly raised money to entertain. He gave Tang a list and said that he had paid a certain amount of money on his behalf. Tang gave him the money. Jia also produced a fake letter of appointment. Tang, not knowing what to do, took it to the designated office. He found out that there was already a county magistrate in the county and that there had been no transfer. Tang realized that he had been deceived. He quickly returned to Hangzhou to find Jia, but he had disappeared. Filled with anger and frustration, he thought that he had no face to see Jiangdong again and had the sudden impulse to end his life. He hired a boat from the Lakeside to the Three Pools Mirroring the Moon and drowned himself. Alas, how unjust!

A Record of Decorative Thieves in Paris 166

— Wu Yuying

Paris, the capital of France, is the birthplace of the world's new fashions. Each well-known new fashion company employs experts who painstakingly work to create various ingenious and artistic clothing. People all over Europe and the United States compete to imitate them. However, recently there has been a discovery of decorative thieves who steal their new designs and make copies. The impact on the business of the new fashion companies is not small. Now what is a decorative thief, let me introduce it as follows:

Most of the so-called decorative thieves are Americans. They frequently visit various new fashion companies in Paris, and all of them are acquainted with each other. Over time, these people came up with a strange idea. If they see a new design of clothing displayed in the window, they immediately draw it as a register. They then rush to London, New York, Hollywood and make copies in the same way. They boast about how new the styles are and how well the sizes fit. Relying on these new outfits, the profit is tripled. By the time representatives from new fashion companies bring new outfits to these cities, their business has already been taken away by these people. The new fashion companies are concerned that if this continues, they will suffer immeasurable losses. They then banded together to find ways to deal with the problem. However, everyone can imitate the styles of new clothes. Therefore, they cannot prosecute these people by law. Then they had to seek passive resistance, and the new fashion companies in Paris put up signs on the decorations of each store, saying "Imitating our new clothing styles is the same as stealing. Customers who want to see the new clothes, please come inside. We cannot put the clever new clothes in the window, for fear of being imitated by decorative thieves." As a result, various new clothes no longer dared to be displayed as window decorations and were hidden in the inner room. Even if there were decorative thieves who did not know better and asked to see the new clothes, hoping to imitate them, they were rejected. Only distinguished customers were allowed to see the truth. From then on, the decorative thieves had nowhere to apply their skills.

On Xun Huisheng's Records 167

— She Yu

Bored during the long summer, I use records to pass the time. I have compiled a list of Xun Huisheng's records released by various companies, as well as those that have not yet been released, with criticisms attached. Pathé Records has three records: "Yu Tang Chun," "West Lake Lord," and "Fanjiang Pass Intoxication." "Drunkenness" is the best of these. Gaoting Records has three and a half records: "Filial Piety Festival," "Hongni Pass," "Stabbing Tang Mu," "Tianwang Yu Tang Chun," and "Hongluan Joy." "Yu Tang Chun" has the most complete sentences and is the most coherent. "Mu Tianwang" is the best at conveying the thoughts of the lines. Beikai Records has seven records: "Liu Rushi," "Hairpin Phoenix," "Yu Tang Chun," "Hongliu Village," "Little Shepherd Boy," "Fragrant Silk Belt," and "Danqing Yin." ("Danqing Yin" has not yet been released. It is a four-line Xipi slow board, with a new, stable tune, achieving a moderate and upright style.) Among them, "Little Shepherd Boy" is the best-selling. Also, the lyrics and melody of "Hairpin Phoenix" are unique, integrating Kunqu opera, similar to string music, and quite pleasant to listen to. The company's legal collection and production can especially enhance its color. Victory Records has three records: "Wandering Tears," "Iron Bow Marriage," "Lantern Riddle," and "Jealous Wife." (Recently, they have continued to collect three records: "Geng Niang," "Thirteenth Sister," "Lantern Riddle," "Pansi Cave," and "Hairpin Phoenix." Their sample pieces have all been listened to. "Geng Niang," "Lantern Riddle," and "Hairpin Phoenix" all use the best two-six of the anti-Xipi. The collection and production is also better than before.) "Iron Bow Marriage," "South Bangzi," and "Wandering Tears Erhuang" are the best of these. Kaiming Records has three records: "Gou Guanniang," "Geng Niang," "Fish Algae Palace," and "Treasure Chest." ("Treasure Chest" has not yet been released. The sung Siping tune uses many unusual peaks in the ups and downs.) "Fish Algae Palace" and the lines of "Xun Guanniang" are the best of these. This company was established later, and its collection and production also have advantages. The sound is high and bright, and there seems to be no damage to the film quality. Dachina has six records: "Thirteenth Period," "Hongluan Joy," "Yu Tang Chun," "Cuiping Mountain," and "Drunk Spilling to Relatives' Homes." "Bang Da" is best in narration, and Cuiping Mountain is spiritually satisfying. His speech when visiting relatives and family is clear. He has achieved the effect of banner women who were very adept with the language. I put Yu Tang Chun together and the set is now complete with works from Baidai, Beikai and Gaoting. In summary, Hui Sheng has a total of fifty-seven records to date, including those that have not yet been released. I am recording this for the enjoyment of fellow record enthusiasts.

The Origins of the French Concession in Shanghai (Part 1) 168

— Ji Ping, translated from the North China Herald Weekly

The first foreigners to come to Shanghai were not French. It was not until 1847, when the Frenchman Montigny came to Shanghai as the French consular representative, that the French had a presence. At that time, business was quite slow, and there were only a few Catholic priests stationed here. Montigny was a man of talent and made many plans for French enterprises in China. Not long after his arrival in Shanghai, the first Frenchman came here to do business. This man, named Remy, was in the business of clocks and watches and foreign wine. After his arrival, the French Consul Montigny asked the Chinese authorities to grant a piece of land to the French. Montigny was deeply concerned that the small French businesses would be overshadowed by British and American businesses. The Chinese government granted a small piece of land. On May 18, 1862, the French Municipal Council was established, with Edan Moore as consul. At that time, the British consul opposed the establishment of the French Municipal Council because it was inconsistent with the Shanghai Land Regulations signed by the treaty countries and the Chinese government. But the French ignored it. At that time, all foreign businesses in Shanghai were in the British Concession. The newly established French Municipal Council had a small annual income. The 1865 budget estimated that the total income would be 103,000 taels of taxes. However, 48,000 taels of this came from license taxes from opium dens, brothels, and gambling houses. At that time, brothels and gambling houses in other concessions did not require licenses or pay taxes. Litigation in the French Concession was also handled well. However, one incident is enough to prove that the French were unwilling to cooperate with other concessions. In 1865, an American was murdered by a Frenchman on a British ship. The ship was docked in Ningbo. The British did not request a trial. The French Consul did not notify the American Consul when questioning the murderer. Perhaps he would have presented evidence. After the interrogation, the murderer was released. The intention of the French authorities in Shanghai was to recognize the French Concession as a permanently ceded territory. The French Consul General was the head of the concession. The Municipal Council was merely an advisory body directly under his jurisdiction. The French Municipal Council had no real power. This can be seen from past events. Whenever the Municipal Council disagreed with the Consul General, he would resolutely dissolve it. The police and volunteer corps were also under his jurisdiction to protect it. The current Consul General is Mr. Gao Zhai Lin.

When Montigny asked the Chinese government to cede land, the power of French Catholicism was gradually stabilizing. The cathedral was built in Xujiahui. The priests also built residences there. They have not been moved to this day. At that time, Chinese officials believed that the harm of Catholic forces to the country was far greater than the opium and merchants in the French Concession. The officials were very angry about this. The church was robbed, and many priests were killed. There was a convent in Xujiahui that did relief work. At that time, superstitious Chinese people threw stones at its windows and broke into the door, threatening them with death. As a result, relief work could not be carried out smoothly. The Xujiahui Catholic Church ran an orphanage. As a result, there were also martyrs. At that time, the Chinese did not know what the French were trying to do. Today, the orphanage houses hundreds of homeless children and teaches them the best crafts.

Heart's Warmth (261) 169

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Thirteen: Who Unintentionally Sows Fortune and Gains a Diamond Ring? Only This Predestined Relationship Inspires a Song of Golden Threads.

In the past, when women who had married returned to the stage, there was often one condition: they were not allowed to use their former names. It was as if they had given their bodies to him, and even their names belonged to him. If they were divorced and returned to the stage, they could no longer use their old brand. This seemed to be a matter of face. In reality, the cicada shedding its shell and moving to another branch still makes the same noise. Forbidding the use of the old name seemed like a self-deceiving act. Therefore, later on, people didn't bother with it so much. Some women who remarried and returned to the stage often hated the mercilessness of the anvil. They deliberately embedded the surname and name of the man they married into their flower banners, such as marrying someone surnamed Yu and calling themselves Yu Ji, or marrying someone surnamed Xie and changing their name to Xie… and so on. However, they thought that there were many concubines, like swallows on the beams, let them come and go as they pleased. It was just the way things were, and there was nothing strange about it. But there was a type of woman who, after marrying someone and coming out again, actually had a better life than before, with the feeling of ascending the dragon gate and increasing their reputation tenfold. Especially the concubines of wealthy people; if they ever came out again, it would cause a sensation. Marrying a wealthy person seemed to give them a new glorious title. The more titles they had, the more their reputation increased, like the politicians of recent times. They were officials during the late Qing Dynasty, and they are officials during the Republic of China. They are in the limelight under the warlord government, and they are in the limelight under the National Government. To the guests, they are like palace ladies from the Tianbao era, hearing about the Kaiyuan era. They also know that the wealthy man's favorite would not dare to neglect them. Therefore, Zuo Shichen asked, "So, Cuiyun has come out this time..." She said shyly, "It's not good." She said she didn't have many old customers. She said it was embarrassing to see the old customers. The day before yesterday, she said to me, "Ah Bao, if you see so and so, please give them a message for me." I said I hadn't bumped into them on the stage. Today is very coincidental, I bumped into you. Are you the host here? You are an old friend of Third Sister. Please help her. Burning incense should be done in a ruined temple." Ah Bao's series of words left Zuo Shichen speechless. Seeing that the gambling ticket of Jiao Chan Nong had been issued, she went to the neighboring seat to socialize with the guests. In less than three minutes, she ran back and said, "Third Sister is coming. Tell her that Ah Bao from Zuo Cuiyun has been here. I have several stage performances and can't wait for her any longer." With that, she took the young gentleman and left. Ten minutes later, Cuiyun, who had changed her name to Chan Nong, came. When Zuo Shichen saw her, he couldn't help but be shocked, thinking that he hadn't seen her for only three or four years, how could she have aged so much? Zuo Shichen almost shouted "Ah ya!" He thought that her age was at most twenty-four or five years old. Could it be true what people say about the age of a beauty, that ten years is a lifetime, from fifteen to twenty-five years old, she has already entered the period of decline? But I have seen people of twenty-four or five years old who are as youthful as girls of eighteen or nineteen.

Weekly News Amidst the Wild Fall in US Cotton 179

New York telegram on the 22nd reports the cotton market situation for the week: The cotton price fell low in the initial stage of this week. Because the actual situation has increased, the market price has rebounded, but the rebound is weak. The demand has shrunk. There have been continuous showers in several cotton belt areas, and Oklahoma has received timely rain, but the rainfall in Tulsa is still insufficient. Some people believe that the eastern cotton production in Alabama has increased, but the cotton production west of the state has decreased since August 1. There is no definite grasp on the situation of cotton production at the end of August and the increase or decrease in figures. Generally, the opinion seems to be that the expected cotton production may not decrease. The short party believes that the numbers shown must be below 14 million bales to stimulate general buying when new cotton is gradually increasing on the market. The weather is hot and the cotton is harvested early. Colleagues expect that the new cotton on the market will suddenly increase as a result, and more people who sell short can immediately be absorbed. This kind of doubt is the basis for predicting that the market price will be lower. Some of the recent cotton in the southwest is said to be needed to cope with Chen Hua's contract. Inside and outside the garden, colleagues have slightly purchased. Although the current popularity is waiting and watching, it is much more direct than before. Some cotton merchants anticipate that the power to resist prices will be greater, but the short party's arrogance is still quite fierce.

It is also reported that the current price has attracted the attention of some yarn factories. There is a slight accumulation of long-term contracts in the south, but the movement of new flowers on the market in the future, the limited short-term demand, and the general state of commercial decline are now obstacles to speculative purchases. Rain has been seen in many places in the southwest, but the rain in Texas and western Oklahoma is small and not universal and not sufficient. The market popularity is sometimes trending towards the short side. The weekend statistics are listed on the left (unit: thousand bales).

Foreign Rice Sales Stagnant, Market Weak 181

Yesterday, the foreign rice market remained weak, and due to stagnant sales, a turnaround was difficult. However, Tianjin, which had been under strict prohibition of shipments for a long time, suddenly appeared in the market with 300 bags of No. 1 Saigon rice, priced at 16 yuan. This rice was reported to be loaded for export to Tianjin on the same day. Since the Tianjin merchants have the appetite for it, the market seems poised for a turnaround. However, the rice market in that area has long been dominated by Japanese merchants and Saigon direct shipments, resulting in low prices, leaving no foothold for Shanghai merchants. Therefore, trading is difficult to increase. This shipment seems to be a trial run. Moreover, the quota for the opening of the Shanghai rice market is very large, and it is rumored that a small number have already been shipped in advance from Saigon. In addition, there were transactions in rural areas, with 300 bags of Mindang rice priced at 15 yuan and 2 jiao, 300 bags of small Jiaoci rice priced at 14 yuan and a half, and 300 bags of Kekan rice priced at 15 yuan and 2 jiao and a half.

Wheat Market: Futures Weak, Spot Lively 183
