Silk and Tea 184

Anhui Dried Cocoons Opening Prices Look Weak

Affected by Japanese cocoons invading the market, prices are generally falling by four to five liang.

This year, the spring and summer cocoons in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces were poor, and the raw materials were scarce, so the cocoon prices rose. The prices of Anhui dried cocoons were also lively. However, after a large number of Japanese cocoons were shipped to Shanghai at low prices, the Chinese cocoons were greatly affected. Yesterday, Ding Yu Jin Datong sold 185 dan of spring dried cocoons inside the port for only 155 liang (640 jin, converted), a drop of four to five liang compared to before. If more Japanese cocoons continue to be shipped to Shanghai, the Anhui cocoon market will become even weaker.

The Arts

Recent German Literary Scene 205

— Ming

Most of the novels recently published in Germany can be classified as social novels, because these works describe various aspects of German social life after the end of the Great War. They can serve as a very useful index to the latest trends in modern German thought and morality. In such novels, the issue of relationships between the sexes naturally occupies the first place among the themes used by writers.

Stefan Zweig’s recent work is also like this. Es Ist Zeit is the latest installment of the Roland novel series. The central figure, of course, is still Roland, as in the previous installments. Although this novel series is too long and too complex, it is a detailed record of German intellectual and social life since the European War. This latest installment writes about a kind of reaction that has recently occurred in Germany, a reaction against the Futility faction and the moral laxity of young people. Originally, Germany, since the Great War, has suffered the humiliation of enemy occupation of important cities. A group of young people are mostly spiritually decadent, grief-stricken, and desperate, thus giving rise to a decadent and cynical attitude of "a merry life while life is here." Thus, the so-called Futility Doctrine was created. This kind of doctrine was once very popular in Germany, but recently, as Germany's vitality gradually recovered and the spirit of the nation gradually rose, there was a very powerful resistance to this self-abandonment and willingness to fall. Zweig's new work writes about the struggle between these two factions. This novel is not only a very interesting social snapshot, but also contains a shocking criminal plot: an old rake, who is very influential in the upper middle class and has committed many evils against the young girls in this social stratum, is murdered. Suspicion of murder falls on a young writer. Although this young writer is also a member of the Futility faction and seems to be a comrade of the old rake, he is still suspected of murder because he once openly denounced the old devil's crimes and said that the old devil's death could rid society of a scourge. Most of this novel narrates how this suspicion hangs over him, unable to be shaken off, but later a girl who has already escaped is proven to be the real murderer, so he is acquitted.

Heinrich Mann, Thomas Mann's older brother, is also an old writer. He has recently published a collection of short stories entitled Sie Sind Jung, in which several stories are about the experiences, interests, strengths, and weaknesses of young German men and women. The best one is about a married man who is morally lax and hypocritically treats everything. Who knows, later his son also uses this kind of unrestrained hypocrisy to deal with him. This short story is terribly strong.

Hans Sochaczwewer, the author of Menschen Nachdem Kriege, appears to be a young man from his writing. This book presents two kinds of Germans in contrast, these two kinds of Germans who have gained their different views on life after the Great War, a kind of model in which all his ideals have been shattered and his patriotism has been overturned. Although his family life is relatively peaceful, even this cannot prevent him from feeling that being a human being is meaningless. The other type is his friend, who is completely different from him, who regards Germany's defeat and revolution as the beginning of a new book, feeling that there is still a good sequel for his country or for himself personally. He lives in peace and contentment, working as a screenwriter and having a romantic affair with a young Romanian woman. The book writes his character very well. This book is not a mature work, but it is worth reading.

Historical Novelist Walter Von Molo 206

Walter Von Molo does not act as a historical novelist in his new book, Die Scheipung. He abandons the historical themes he had previously used to great success and instead uses divorce as a theme. This novel is an interesting study of an unhappy marriage that is ruined by the wife. She cannot adapt herself to her husband's temperament and finds that having children can provide more helpers to oppose her man. She believes that marriage is only a temporary union with no special responsibilities or obligations. This is her own assumed theorem, but she then acts according to her theorem. From the lines of this novel, it seems to be in favor of monogamy. From the point of view of its expression of social trends, it can be compared with Zweig's novel. However, both in form and style, this novel is far inferior to Zweig's new work.

Rudolf Borchardt's new book, Dao Hoffnungslose Gescht, is a collection of short stories entirely on the subject of relationships between men and women. The longest one is actually a male study. This man is marrying for special purposes, written very exquisitely and interestingly, reminiscent of Henry James, who focuses on technique, and the style of writing is very mature. This is not beyond everyone's expectations, because Borchardt is one of the best writers in modern Germany and is highly regarded in his own country, but not many people know him abroad. However, writers of similar status to him

Bruns Grank is very famous abroad. His long short story PoliticalNovelle satirizes the famous French diplomat Briand, and especially caused a sensation in Europe and the United States. His recent work Der Magier is also a novella. The magician mentioned in the title is a stage director, a genius in directing dramas. After his successful performances in Austria, he suddenly disappeared, and it is said that he went to somewhere in the United States to perform the surprisingly talented Negro drama. This novel is also well written, and Frank's strengths are revealed.

The Experimental Female Writer

Ｖicki Baum is a new writer who has recently caused a sensation in Germany. She is not only a believer in realism, but also a practitioner of experimentalism, because before writing her latest novel, Menschen inHotel, she went to a hotel in Berlin to work as a waitress for six weeks in order to obtain the truth of life in a large hotel. There are very few writers as sincere and patient as she is. The background of this novel is a large hotel in Berlin, Germany. The characters in the book are all guests in the hotel. After the publication of this novel, it was a great success and was even adapted into a drama, which was performed in Berlin and then in Vienna and other major European cities, so Wang Jibao immediately became a popular writer. She is a trained musician and the wife of the bandleader of the Berlin National Opera House, and has traveled alone to North Africa on a sex adventure.

Book Review

Confessions 209

— Wenzhi

By Guo Zixiong

In fact, which young person in this era would not be attacked by depression? To be honest, unless they are generally slow-thinking and numb-nerved, they will not be affected by the arrival of depression and only know how to live a numb life in a muddle-headed way. If there is such a thing as inspiration in the world, then the depression of young people can never be eliminated and will often grow. This is really because the desire of young people to move upward is too high. However, what we require is that in the progress of life, although we encounter environmental obstacles, oppression, and constraints, and feel pain and boredom, the will to survive must be strong, and we must struggle at all times and fight at all times in the vortex of pain and boredom. Struggle to fight the forces of obstruction, oppression, and restraint, fully exert the requirements of life, and seek victory. Only in this way can the meaning of valuable life be reflected in literary and artistic works, which is the work we need. However, when we turn to works that express this kind of modern young people, we are all disappointed. Most of them are just a kind of listless and decadent unconscious cry, just venting the anger in the heart and expressing dissatisfaction with the status quo, without the ambition to move towards the light. This kind of cry only forms a moan, nothing more than a dry cry of a defeated soldier who is afraid of battle. It is still far from the field of literature and art.

This book "Confessions" is also a work of this kind of injury in the mold. In order to endure the urging of the soul, tonight I want to draw a flower autograph in front of you, a confession (one page). This is probably the author's attitude. It contains eleven essays: Confessions (1), Confessions (2), Who to Blame? Are You Hiding from Me? Farewell to the Passing Years, the Boredom of Modern People, My Elder Brother, One Night in Wushan, In Lushan. The common point of each article is the confession-style telling of inner depression and the shackles of the environment encountered.

The biggest symbol of the modern young people's greatest depression is naturally the question of love. In fact, love gives young people not victory but sorrow, not a paean but a curse. However, when the buds of youth are bright and beautiful, who can be exempt? If the feelings of human beings can be extinguished for a while, that's all. However, this is definitely impossible. Therefore, most of the cries of young people today that are reflected in literary and artistic works are curses on the manipulation of this love journey. Here, Confessions is also unable to escape the exception. I pick up my pen, dipping it in ink mixed with tears and with heavy sorrow, to write to you, regardless of whether you accept my intention or not and whether you want to listen to my incoherent words. I finally did this. If I have committed a crime, then you are my God. I hope you will forgive me as you forgive other people, and I hope you will be merciful and allow me to lie beside you, close my eyes, and have a sweet dream for a moment, so that my wandering soul can rest temporarily (one page). Because, but after all, I can't forget you. I can't forget you when I'm alive, and I can't forget you when I'm dead. I'm not afraid that one day my bones will turn into dust, but every tiny molecule in that dust still contains your existence, just like a soldier who has fallen on the battlefield, although his bones are already cold and his heart can no longer move, the wisp-like soul still cannot forget the country he came from (nine pages). Although he himself understands that he has taken the wrong path (two pages), emotion is, after all, a subtle thing. It seems ordinary, but it is also mysterious. It seems mysterious, but it is also ordinary. Moreover, the psychological state of young people is mostly like this. You are a lamp in the dark night, on the long road, in front of me. As long as I have you, I am not afraid of wind, rain, jackals, and tigers howling, or the violent forest waves caused by big trees. I am not afraid. Life is two eyes, and ideals are a lamp. With a lamp, the eyes can see. With an ideal, one can be a person. At this time, I can still muster the courage to move forward, just because I have this lamp to illuminate me in the dark night and on the dark long road (13 pages). These various fantasies that are cherished, where can we talk about courage and enthusiasm? It is just like this kind of meaningless moan, please accept this shadow of mine and do not forget that I, such a flower, once bloomed in the garden of your life, and at the same time, I can only be like Jingwei, carrying stones and branches to throw into the vast East China Sea year after year (14 pages). Oh, is this the so-called value of pursuit? Value?

Who to blame is also the same. Who cannot be blamed? He can only blame himself for putting new grape juice into old leather bags. Repent! It is useless. The withered buds and fallen leaves can never grow back on the branches. Was it wrong? Let it be wrong. I want to be wrong. I want to be wrong. In the end, it is a fork in the road. I have to go. I want to go to its end (15 pages). All illusory demands are nothing more than not forgetting that in this vast world there is such a me. He loves you, but he does not necessarily want you to love him. You hate him, but he does not necessarily hate you (17 pages). Although I think that I should not let down the blue sky above my head and the earth under my feet, to be a person must be a person and must be serious, and admit that if I do not climb to the top of the peak, I should not have started walking in the first place. Why retreat halfway? (21 pages) But in the end, there is no definite will.

Manuscript Guidelines for Book and Newspaper Reviews 210

(1) The text should be limited to introducing the latest publications, both domestic and foreign. Except for literary works, all books and newspapers on politics, economics, law, science, education, etc., are included in the reviews. However, frivolous books and newspapers will not be reviewed.

(2) Illustrations should be limited to recent works by new artists, both domestic and foreign, and related illustrations to the text.

(3) Manuscripts concerning textual research or studies of ancient Chinese books will not be published.

(4) Illustrations and photographs should be limited to those related to the text.

(5) Each article should not exceed 3,000 characters at most.

(6) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(7) Do not write the manuscript horizontally. Avoid cursive writing. Western text should be abbreviated where possible. If it is absolutely necessary to quote the original text, it must be attached below the translation.

(8) Do not use blue ink to draw illustrations, and do not use colored paper. Use white paper with black ink.

(9) Please indicate "Book and Newspaper Review Section" for incoming manuscripts.

(10) Submitted manuscripts will not be returned whether published or not. If a return is required, please state so in advance and include sufficient postage.

(11) Remuneration for articles is divided into three categories: three yuan, two yuan, and one yuan per thousand characters. The same applies to illustrations and photographs per piece. Special manuscripts will be remunerated separately.

Page 30

Are you evading too? Seeming to be poured from the same mold, sweet memories of the past only bring futile sorrow. When life's boat hits fate's reef, living is certainly good, but dying is also proper. If the past karma is worth cherishing, then please remember me, remember you, a dream once experienced. If our encounter was unfortunate, then please forget me, as if forgetting someone insignificant. (Page 31) That's all.

Rejection is expressing that one's dreamlike past, foggy future, coupled with a gray present, is my life. (Page 37) So please forgive me, girl. I dare not exchange your true feelings with a false heart, nor accept your warm kisses with cold lips. I do not wish to squander the remaining days of my youth in your arms, therefore I must disappoint your sea-like depth and purity. (Page 33) What unsteady thoughts those are!

Only the fleeting water is truly saddened. The past life is a dim painting. (Page 52) Indeed, if life's journey were all smooth and level, without any steepness or ruggedness, and if there were no dramatic changes in life or strong blows to the soul during the decades of living, then even if one could spend the twilight years quietly, the meaning of being human and the value of life would inevitably be lost and completely extinguished. (Page 43) Unfortunately, although our author knows that the road ahead is at its end, why should I bother seeking a path out of the depths of despair? (Page 47) Regarding his own way out, he is still more hesitant and desolate than a wild goose carrying an arrow in the west wind. (Page 53) Alas, the depression of a neurotic youth probably symbolizes the majority.

"Four Years," is my favorite among them. Indeed, turning back to ask oneself, what has these four years of university life actually given me? (Page 57) I believe this is something no one can answer. Originally, when university life is about to end, two opposing feelings must coexist in everyone's heart: aversion and nostalgia. However, it is ultimately futile. Eventually, people put on square hats and black robes, accepting the vain degree with dignity, walking out of the school gate and stepping onto another path of life, shouldering the responsibility of being human. (Page 62) As for what happens after entering society, that is truly uncertain.

The boredom of modern people is truly a psychological sketch of the sick of the century, lacking courage towards life, society, and the nation. (Page 68) Alas, what kind of acupuncture treatment should be applied to restore them to their original vitality? It really cannot be obtained. Why do young people only know how to curse fate?

My elder brother's expressive power is excellent, with sincere feelings and heartfelt grief. But the sobbing of women and the crying of children cannot awaken your spirit in the tomb. You are gone, and from now on, all the changes in the human world, the temptations of sound and color, can no longer enter your heart. You are gone, no longer caring about the blooming and withering of flowers, the waxing and waning of the moon, the green and yellow of grass, the growth and fall of leaves. You are gone. (Page 82) In these few plain sentences, how much mourning is filled! Especially at this sorrowful time of brotherly death, how can one avoid reminiscence and inner lamentation?

"One Night in Wushan" and "In Lushan" are travelogues that cannot escape the style of a frustrated scholar, lamenting when facing beautiful scenery.

The writing in this collection is very beautiful and vivid, with few carved sentences. It is a pity that it is too much of an unconscious venting for the individual. The reason for this is the lack of ability to develop and express one's own life's demands, thus falling into unintentional sentimentality. This may be due to the author's life experience, but this point should be overcome with effort. You should know that our nation has suffered misunderstanding to this point, and this aspect of weakness and decline, the so-called sentimental and neurotic tendencies, has also affected many people.

The Catastrophe of Xiang River 211

Changsha was attacked and entered by the Communist army on July 27th. All government offices and prosperous markets were turned into scorched earth. It was not until August 5th that they retreated. The people were unable to escape due to the suddenness of the event, and the involvement of foreign industries has aroused international negotiations.

Vocational Education 212

The China Vocational Education Society was jointly founded by educators from the North and South in May of the sixth year of the Republic of China. Its purposes are (1) to promote and improve vocational education; (2) to improve general education to prepare people for life; and (3) to guide occupational improvement so that the unemployed have employment and the employed enjoy their work. Since its establishment, in addition to investigation, research, lectures, and guidance, it has established the China Vocational School, initially offering courses in ironwork, woodwork, button making, and sericulture, as well as a vocational education instructor training course and a preparatory course for studying in France through diligence and frugality. Currently, it offers courses in mechanical engineering, civil engineering, commerce, and the Shanghai Central Woodworking Classroom, with a total of over 700 students. Over 1,000 students have graduated in past years. It is affiliated with the China Ironworks Factory and the China Sericulture Factory. It jointly operates the Zhenjiang Women's Vocational School with local people in Zhenjiang, offering courses in sericulture with over 100 students. It also established the Sanyi Mulberry and Silk Farm in Qiaotou Town near Zhenjiang. In the vocational specialized night school affiliated with the Society, there are general bookkeeping courses, bank bookkeeping courses, survey statistics science courses, and Chinese typing courses. It also runs a worker's supplementary morning school and a common school. In recent years, to promote rural education, it has designated a rural area of over 2,000 people and 20 square miles in Xugongqiao, Kunshan, Jiangsu Province, to comprehensively improve the countryside, including village administration, agriculture, education, security, construction, and entertainment. It is entrusted by the Jiangsu Provincial Agriculture and Forestry Committee to handle the rural improvement in Huangjia Town, Zhenjiang, with a population of over 5,000 and an area of 53 square miles. The methods are similar to those in Xugongqiao, but with special emphasis on production. The New Agricultural Implement Promotion Office, affiliated with the Society, manufactures and promotes new agricultural implements, guiding farmers to try them out, which has proven effective. The Society also has a service team to enhance the services of mechanical engineering students. The Society also has a vocational guidance office that provides guidance to young men and women on further education and employment, as well as job placement services. Dozens of people receive guidance every day. The Society publishes the "Education and Vocation" monthly magazine, the "Life Weekly," and 460 other special publications. The Society has had over 8,000 members. Recently, due to a lack of teachers, the board of directors and enthusiastic comrades have raised funds to support the Society, so that it can maintain its public mission. What is recorded here is a small part of the Society's activities.

(1) The China Vocational Education Society's new building was inaugurated on July 25th. The five-story building is in Spanish style, with its main entrance at the intersection of Huilong Road and Vallon Road in the French Concession.

(2) One corner of the China Vocational Education Society's office. Mr. Huang Renzhi, the founder, sits in the back, giving instructions.
